Optimize the hiring capability (people, process, technology) needed to plan, execute and measure talent acquisition recruiting activity. Goal is to drive positive results in talent quality, diversity and speed to hire, through leading a team to establish planning processes, understand internal ready &amp; available talent via active database, implement best practices &amp; execute flawless hiring strategies for our clients.

Establishing trust with clients across through proactive solution development, delivery against commitments, and honest, transparent communication.

Capable of working independently with very little direction on complex projects. Initiates new assignments; acts as a facilitator and mentor within project context.<!----></span>
